<pr_description>
[BUG] ACM rejects import of valid certs
## Service

ACM

## AWS API Action

ImportCertificate

## Expected behavior

Successful import

## Actual behavior

HTTP 400 error

ERROR: An error occurred (ValidationException) when calling the ImportCertificate operation: Invalid certificate: Certificate parsing failed: Invalid certificate PEM format

## Reproduction

```bash
# Generate a self-signed cert
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/key.pem -out /tmp/cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null

# This works — direct HTTP with PEM as plain string:
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}"

# This fails — AWS CLI base64-encodes blobs per JSON 1.1 spec:
aws acm import-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate fileb:///tmp/cert.pem \
  --private-key fileb:///tmp/key.pem
```

## Environment

- Floci version / image tag: 1.3.0
- Java SDK version (if applicable): 25
- How you're running Floci: `mvn quarkus:dev`
[BUG] ACM refuses to export an imported cert
## Service

ACM

## AWS API Action

ExportCertificate

## Expected behavior

After importing a user-provided certificate, export certificate should be allowed.

## Actual behavior

operation error ACM: ExportCertificate, https response error StatusCode: 400, RequestID: 4dddfc97-4919-4464-ba80-0a6a90385603, api error ValidationException: Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED

## Reproduction

```bash
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/key.pem -out /tmp/cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null

aws acm import-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate fileb:///tmp/cert.pem \
  --private-key fileb:///tmp/key.pem
For the export bug:

# Import via direct HTTP (workaround for the import bug)
ARN=$(curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}" \
  | jq -r .CertificateArn)

aws acm export-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate-arn "$ARN" \
  --passphrase "test-passphrase"
```

## Environment

- Floci version / image tag: 1.3.0
- Java SDK version (if applicable): 25
- How you're running Floci: `mvn quarkus:dev`

    38	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) {
    39	        return switch (action) {
    40	            case "RequestCertificate" -> handleRequestCertificate(request, region);
    41	            case "DescribeCertificate" -> handleDescribeCertificate(request, region);
    42	            case "GetCertificate" -> handleGetCertificate(request, region);
    43	            case "ListCertificates" -> handleListCertificates(request, region);
    44	            case "DeleteCertificate" -> handleDeleteCertificate(request, region);
    45	            case "ImportCertificate" -> handleImportCertificate(request, region);
    46	            case "ExportCertificate" -> handleExportCertificate(request, region);
    47	            case "AddTagsToCertificate" -> handleAddTagsToCertificate(request, region);
    48	            case "ListTagsForCertificate" -> handleListTagsForCertificate(request, region);
    49	            case "RemoveTagsFromCertificate" -> handleRemoveTagsFromCertificate(request, region);
    50	            case "GetAccountConfiguration" -> handleGetAccountConfiguration(request, region);
    51	            case "PutAccountConfiguration" -> handlePutAccountConfiguration(request, region);
    52	            default -> Response.status(400)
    53	                .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnsupportedOperation", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
    54	                .build();
    55	        };
    56	    }

    58	    private Response handleRequestCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
    59	        String domainName = request.path("DomainName").asText(null);
    60	        if (domainName == null || domainName.isBlank()) {
    61	            return Response.status(400)
    62	                .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("ValidationException",
    63	                    "Value null at 'domainName' failed to satisfy constraint: Member must not be null"))
    64	                .build();
    65	        }
    66	        List<String> sans = parseStringList(request.path("SubjectAlternativeNames"));
    67	        ValidationMethod validationMethod = parseValidationMethod(request.path("ValidationMethod").asText(null));
    68	        String idempotencyToken = request.path("IdempotencyToken").asText(null);
    69	        KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm = KeyAlgorithm.fromAwsName(request.path("KeyAlgorithm").asText(null));
    70	        String certAuthorityArn = request.path("CertificateAuthorityArn").asText(null);
    71	        CertificateOptions options = parseOptions(request.path("Options"));
    72	        Map<String, String> tags = parseTags(request.path("Tags"));
    73	
    74	        Certificate cert = service.requestCertificate(domainName, sans, validationMethod,
    75	            idempotencyToken, keyAlgorithm, certAuthorityArn, options, tags, region);
    76	
    77	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    78	        response.put("CertificateArn", cert.getArn());
    79	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    private Response handleDescribeCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
    83	        String certificateArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText();
    84	        Certificate cert = service.describeCertificate(certificateArn, region);
    85	
    86	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    87	        response.set("Certificate", buildCertificateDetail(cert));
    88	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    private Response handleGetCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
    92	        String certificateArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText();
    93	        Certificate cert = service.getCertificate(certificateArn, region);
    94	
    95	        // AWS returns RequestInProgressException for certificates still pending validation
    96	        if (cert.getStatus() == CertificateStatus.PENDING_VALIDATION) {
    97	            throw new io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.AwsException(
    98	                "RequestInProgressException",
    99	                "The certificate request is in progress. The certificate body is not yet available.",
   100	                400);
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   104	        response.put("Certificate", cert.getCertificateBody());
   105	        if (cert.getCertificateChain() != null) {
   106	            response.put("CertificateChain", cert.getCertificateChain());
   107	        }
   108	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    private Response handleListCertificates(JsonNode request, String region) {
   112	        List<CertificateStatus> statuses = parseCertificateStatuses(request.path("CertificateStatuses"));
   113	        List<KeyAlgorithm> keyTypes = parseKeyTypes(request.path("Includes").path("keyTypes"));
   114	        int maxItems = request.path("MaxItems").asInt(100);
   115	        String nextToken = request.path("NextToken").asText(null);
   116	
   117	        ListResult result = service.listCertificates(statuses, keyTypes, region, maxItems, nextToken);
   118	
   119	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   120	        ArrayNode summaryList = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   121	        for (Certificate cert : result.certificates()) {
   122	            summaryList.add(buildCertificateSummary(cert));
   123	        }
   124	        response.set("CertificateSummaryList", summaryList);
   125	        if (result.nextToken() != null) {
   126	            response.put("NextToken", result.nextToken());
   127	        }
   128	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   129	    }

   131	    private Response handleDeleteCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
   132	        String certificateArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText();
   133	        service.deleteCertificate(certificateArn, region);
   134	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();

   137	    private Response handleImportCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
   138	        String certificate = request.path("Certificate").asText();
   139	        String privateKey = request.path("PrivateKey").asText();
   140	        String chain = request.path("CertificateChain").asText(null);
   141	        String existingArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText(null);
   142	        Map<String, String> tags = parseTags(request.path("Tags"));
   143	
   144	        Certificate cert = service.importCertificate(certificate, privateKey, chain, existingArn, tags, region);
   145	
   146	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   147	        response.put("CertificateArn", cert.getArn());
   148	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   149	    }

   175	        String certificateArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText();
   176	        Map<String, String> tags = service.listTagsForCertificate(certificateArn, region);
   177	
   178	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   179	        ArrayNode tagsArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   180	        for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : tags.entrySet()) {

   183	            tagNode.put("Value", entry.getValue());
   184	            tagsArray.add(tagNode);
   185	        }
   186	        response.set("Tags", tagsArray);
   187	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   188	    }

   190	    private Response handleRemoveTagsFromCertificate(JsonNode request, String region) {
   191	        String certificateArn = request.path("CertificateArn").asText();
   192	        List<Map<String, String>> tagSpecs = new ArrayList<>();
   193	        JsonNode tagsNode = request.path("Tags");
   194	        if (tagsNode.isArray()) {
   195	            for (JsonNode tagNode : tagsNode) {
   196	                Map<String, String> spec = new HashMap<>();
   197	                spec.put("Key", tagNode.path("Key").asText());
   198	                if (tagNode.has("Value")) {
   199	                    spec.put("Value", tagNode.path("Value").asText());
   200	                }
   201	                tagSpecs.add(spec);
   202	            }
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        service.removeTagsFromCertificate(certificateArn, tagSpecs, region);
   206	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
   207	    }

   213	        ObjectNode expiryEvents = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   214	        expiryEvents.put("DaysBeforeExpiry", daysBeforeExpiry);
   215	        response.set("ExpiryEvents", expiryEvents);

   229	    private ObjectNode buildCertificateDetail(Certificate cert) {
   230	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   231	        node.put("CertificateArn", cert.getArn());
   232	        node.put("DomainName", cert.getDomainName());
   233	
   234	        ArrayNode sans = objectMapper.createArrayNode();

   236	            cert.getSubjectAlternativeNames().forEach(sans::add);
   237	        }
   238	        node.set("SubjectAlternativeNames", sans);
   239	        node.set("SubjectAlternativeNameSummaries", sans.deepCopy());
   240	        node.put("HasAdditionalSubjectAlternativeNames", false);
   241	
   242	        node.put("Status", cert.getStatus().name());
   243	        node.put("Type", cert.getType().name());
   244	
   245	        if (cert.getKeyAlgorithm() != null) {
   246	            node.put("KeyAlgorithm", cert.getKeyAlgorithm().getAwsName());
   247	        }
   248	        if (cert.getSignatureAlgorithm() != null) {
   249	            node.put("SignatureAlgorithm", cert.getSignatureAlgorithm());
   250	        }
   251	        if (cert.getSerial() != null) {
   252	            node.put("Serial", cert.getSerial());
   253	        }
   254	        if (cert.getSubject() != null) {
   255	            node.put("Subject", cert.getSubject());
   256	        }
   257	        if (cert.getIssuer() != null) {
   258	            node.put("Issuer", cert.getIssuer());
   259	        }
   260	
   261	        if (cert.getCreatedAt() != null) {
   262	            node.put("CreatedAt", cert.getCreatedAt().toEpochMilli() / 1000.0);
   263	        }
   264	        if (cert.getIssuedAt() != null) {
   265	            node.put("IssuedAt", cert.getIssuedAt().toEpochMilli() / 1000.0);
   266	        }
   267	        if (cert.getImportedAt() != null) {
   268	            node.put("ImportedAt", cert.getImportedAt().toEpochMilli() / 1000.0);
   269	        }
   270	        if (cert.getNotBefore() != null) {
   271	            node.put("NotBefore", cert.getNotBefore().toEpochMilli() / 1000.0);
   272	        }
   273	        if (cert.getNotAfter() != null) {
   274	            node.put("NotAfter", cert.getNotAfter().toEpochMilli() / 1000.0);
   275	        }
   276	
   277	        ArrayNode inUseBy = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   278	        if (cert.getInUseBy() != null) {
   279	            cert.getInUseBy().forEach(inUseBy::add);
   280	        }
   281	        node.set("InUseBy", inUseBy);
   282	
   283	        if (cert.getDomainValidationOptions() != null && !cert.getDomainValidationOptions().isEmpty()) {
   284	            ArrayNode validations = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   285	            for (DomainValidation dv : cert.getDomainValidationOptions()) {
   286	                ObjectNode dvNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   287	                dvNode.put("DomainName", dv.domainName());
   288	                dvNode.put("ValidationDomain", dv.validationDomain());
   289	                dvNode.put("ValidationStatus", dv.validationStatus());
   290	                dvNode.put("ValidationMethod", dv.validationMethod());
   291	                if (dv.resourceRecord() != null) {
   292	                    ObjectNode rrNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   293	                    rrNode.put("Name", dv.resourceRecord().name());
   294	                    rrNode.put("Type", dv.resourceRecord().type());
   295	                    rrNode.put("Value", dv.resourceRecord().value());
   296	                    dvNode.set("ResourceRecord", rrNode);
   297	                }
   298	                validations.add(dvNode);
   299	            }
   300	            node.set("DomainValidationOptions", validations);
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        node.put("RenewalEligibility", "INELIGIBLE");
   304	
   305	        ArrayNode keyUsages = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   306	        ObjectNode ku1 = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   307	        ku1.put("Name", "DIGITAL_SIGNATURE");
   308	        keyUsages.add(ku1);
   309	        ObjectNode ku2 = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   310	        ku2.put("Name", "KEY_ENCIPHERMENT");
   311	        keyUsages.add(ku2);
   312	        node.set("KeyUsages", keyUsages);
   313	
   314	        ArrayNode extKeyUsages = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   315	        ObjectNode eku1 = objectMapper.createObjectNode();

   317	        eku1.put("OID", "1.3.6.1.5.5.7.3.1");

    28	/**
    29	 * ACM (AWS Certificate Manager) service implementation for the local emulator.
    30	 *
    31	 * <p>Provides X.509 certificate management operations compatible with the AWS ACM API,
    32	 * including certificate request, import, export, and lifecycle management.</p>
    33	 *
    34	 * @see <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/acm/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html">AWS ACM API Reference</a>
    35	 */
    36	@ApplicationScoped
    37	public class AcmService {
    38	
    39	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(AcmService.class);
    40	    private static final int MAX_TAGS = 50;
    41	    private static final int MAX_TAG_KEY_LENGTH = 128;
    42	    private static final int MAX_TAG_VALUE_LENGTH = 256;
    43	    private static final int MAX_SANS = 100;
    44	    private static final int MAX_DOMAIN_LENGTH = 253;
    45	    private static final SecureRandom SECURE_RANDOM = new SecureRandom();

    48	    private final CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator;
    49	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    50	    private final int validationWaitSeconds;
    51	    private final AtomicInteger accountDaysBeforeExpiry = new AtomicInteger(45);
    52	    private final AtomicBoolean securityWarningLogged = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    53	
    54	    /**
    55	     * Idempotency token cache using lazy expiration (1-hour TTL).
    56	     *
    57	     * <p>Design decision: Using ConcurrentHashMap with timestamp-based entries
    58	     * instead of Caffeine or scheduled cleanup. This matches moto's approach
    59	     * (see moto/acm/models.py:478-505) where expired entries are removed on
    60	     * lookup. No background thread needed - acceptable for emulator workloads.</p>
    61	     *
    62	     * @see <a href="https://github.com/getmoto/moto/blob/main/moto/acm/models.py">moto ACM</a>
    63	     */
    64	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, IdempotencyTokenEntry> idempotencyTokenIndex = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    65	
    66	    @Inject
    67	    public AcmService(StorageFactory factory, CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator,
    68	                      EmulatorConfig config, RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    69	        this(factory.create("acm", "acm-certificates.json",
    70	                new TypeReference<Map<String, Certificate>>() {}),
    71	            certificateGenerator,
    72	            regionResolver,
    73	            config.services().acm().validationWaitSeconds());
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    AcmService(StorageBackend<String, Certificate> store, CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator,
    77	               RegionResolver regionResolver, int validationWaitSeconds) {
    78	        this.store = store;
    79	        this.certificateGenerator = certificateGenerator;
    80	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    81	        this.validationWaitSeconds = validationWaitSeconds;
    82	
    83	        // Validate Root CA resource availability
    84	        validateRootCaResource();
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    /**
    88	     * Log security warning once on first certificate creation/import.
    89	     * Uses AtomicBoolean to ensure thread-safe single logging.
    90	     */
    91	    private void logSecurityWarningOnce() {
    92	        if (securityWarningLogged.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
    93	            LOG.warn("SECURITY WARNING: ACM emulator stores private keys in plaintext. " +
    94	                     "This is acceptable for local development but NOT for production use.");
    95	        }
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    private void validateRootCaResource() {
    99	        try (InputStream is = getClass().getResourceAsStream("/certs/amazon-root-ca.pem")) {
   100	            if (is == null) {
   101	                LOG.warn("Amazon Root CA certificate not found at /certs/amazon-root-ca.pem - " +
   102	                         "certificate chains will be empty");
   103	            } else {
   104	                LOG.info("Amazon Root CA certificate loaded successfully");
   105	            }
   106	        } catch (IOException e) {
   107	            LOG.warnv("Failed to validate Root CA resource: {0}", e.getMessage());
   108	        }
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    // ============ RequestCertificate ============
   112	
   113	    public Certificate requestCertificate(String domainName, List<String> sans, ValidationMethod validationMethod,
   114	                                          String idempotencyToken, KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm,
   115	                                          String certAuthorityArn, CertificateOptions options,
   116	                                          Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   117	        logSecurityWarningOnce();
   118	        validateDomainName(domainName);
   119	        validateSans(sans);
   120	        if (tags != null) {
   121	            validateTags(tags);
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        KeyAlgorithm alg = keyAlgorithm != null ? keyAlgorithm : KeyAlgorithm.RSA_2048;
   125	
   126	        // Check idempotency with parameter validation
   127	        if (idempotencyToken != null && !idempotencyToken.isEmpty()) {
   128	            int requestHash = computeRequestHash(domainName, sans, alg);
   129	            Optional<Certificate> existing = findByIdempotencyToken(idempotencyToken, region, requestHash);
   130	            if (existing.isPresent()) {
   131	                return existing.get();
   132	            }
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        String certId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   136	        String arn = buildCertificateArn(region, certId);
   137	
   138	        // Determine certificate type and initial status
   139	        CertificateType type;
   140	        CertificateStatus status;
   141	        if (certAuthorityArn != null && !certAuthorityArn.isEmpty()) {
   142	            type = CertificateType.PRIVATE;
   143	            status = CertificateStatus.ISSUED;
   144	        } else {
   145	            type = CertificateType.AMAZON_ISSUED;
   146	            status = validationWaitSeconds > 0 ? CertificateStatus.PENDING_VALIDATION : CertificateStatus.ISSUED;
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        // Generate real X.509 certificate
   150	        CertificateGenerator.GeneratedCertificate generated = certificateGenerator.generateCertificate(
   151	            domainName, sans, alg
   152	        );
   153	
   154	        Instant now = Instant.now();
   155	
   156	        Certificate cert = new Certificate();
   157	        cert.setArn(arn);
   158	        cert.setDomainName(domainName);
   159	
   160	        // Use LinkedHashSet for O(1) deduplication while preserving insertion order
   161	        LinkedHashSet<String> allSans = new LinkedHashSet<>();
   162	        allSans.add(domainName);
   163	        if (sans != null) {
   164	            allSans.addAll(sans);
   165	        }
   166	        cert.setSubjectAlternativeNames(new ArrayList<>(allSans));
   167	
   168	        cert.setStatus(status);
   169	        cert.setType(type);
   170	        cert.setValidationMethod(validationMethod != null ? validationMethod : ValidationMethod.DNS);
   171	        cert.setCreatedAt(now);
   172	        cert.setIssuedAt(status == CertificateStatus.ISSUED ? now : null);
   173	        cert.setNotBefore(generated.notBefore());
   174	        cert.setNotAfter(generated.notAfter());
   175	        cert.setSerial(generated.serial());
   176	        cert.setSubject(generated.subject());
   177	        cert.setIssuer(generated.issuer());
   178	        cert.setKeyAlgorithm(alg);
   179	        cert.setSignatureAlgorithm(generated.signatureAlgorithm());
   180	        cert.setCertificateBody(generated.certificatePem());
   181	        cert.setPrivateKey(generated.privateKeyPem());
   182	        cert.setCertificateChain(getAwsRootCa());
   183	        cert.setCertOptions(options != null ? options : CertificateOptions.defaultOptions());
   184	        cert.setCertAuthorityArn(certAuthorityArn);
   185	        cert.setIdempotencyToken(idempotencyToken);
   186	        cert.setTags(tags != null ? new HashMap<>(tags) : new HashMap<>());
   187	
   188	        // Generate domain validation options with correct status based on type
   189	        List<DomainValidation> validations = new ArrayList<>();
   190	        for (String san : allSans) {
   191	            validations.add(generateDomainValidation(san, validationMethod, type));
   192	        }
   193	        cert.setDomainValidationOptions(validations);
   194	
   195	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, certId);
   196	        store.put(storageKey, cert);
   197	
   198	        // Index idempotency token for fast lookups with TTL
   199	        if (idempotencyToken != null && !idempotencyToken.isEmpty()) {
   200	            int requestHash = computeRequestHash(domainName, sans, alg);
   201	            idempotencyTokenIndex.put(region + "::" + idempotencyToken,
   202	                IdempotencyTokenEntry.create(arn, requestHash));
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        LOG.infov("Created certificate: {0} in region {1}", arn, region);
   206	        return cert;
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    // ============ DescribeCertificate ============
   210	
   211	    public Certificate describeCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {
   212	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   213	
   214	        // Check for expiration
   215	        if (cert.isExpired() && cert.getStatus() != CertificateStatus.EXPIRED) {
   216	            cert.setStatus(CertificateStatus.EXPIRED);
   217	            store.put(regionKey(region, cert.extractCertificateId()), cert);
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        return cert;
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    // ============ GetCertificate ============
   224	
   225	    public Certificate getCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {
   226	        return getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    // ============ ListCertificates ============
   230	
   231	    /**
   232	     * Lists certificates with cursor-based pagination.
   233	     *
   234	     * @param statuses Filter by certificate status (null or empty for all)
   235	     * @param keyTypes Filter by key algorithm (null or empty for all)
   236	     * @param region AWS region
   237	     * @param maxItems Maximum items per page (default 100)
   238	     * @param nextToken Cursor for next page (null for first page)
   239	     * @return ListResult containing certificates and optional nextToken
   240	     */
   241	    public ListResult listCertificates(List<CertificateStatus> statuses, List<KeyAlgorithm> keyTypes,
   242	                                       String region, int maxItems, String nextToken) {
   243	        int limit = maxItems > 0 ? Math.min(maxItems, 1000) : 100;
   244	        String lastArn = decodeToken(nextToken);
   245	
   246	        List<Certificate> allCerts = store.scan(k -> true).stream()
   247	            .filter(c -> c.getArn().contains(":acm:" + region + ":"))
   248	            .filter(c -> statuses == null || statuses.isEmpty() || statuses.contains(c.getStatus()))
   249	            .filter(c -> keyTypes == null || keyTypes.isEmpty() || keyTypes.contains(c.getKeyAlgorithm()))
   250	            .sorted(Comparator.comparing(Certificate::getArn))
   251	            .collect(Collectors.toList());
   252	
   253	        // Find starting position based on cursor
   254	        int startIndex = 0;
   255	        if (lastArn != null) {
   256	            for (int i = 0; i < allCerts.size(); i++) {
   257	                if (allCerts.get(i).getArn().compareTo(lastArn) > 0) {
   258	                    startIndex = i;
   259	                    break;
   260	                }
   261	                if (i == allCerts.size() - 1) {
   262	                    startIndex = allCerts.size(); // All items before cursor
   263	                }
   264	            }
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        // Get page
   268	        List<Certificate> page = allCerts.stream()
   269	            .skip(startIndex)
   270	            .limit(limit)
   271	            .collect(Collectors.toList());
   272	
   273	        // Determine if there are more items
   274	        String newNextToken = null;
   275	        if (startIndex + limit < allCerts.size() && !page.isEmpty()) {
   276	            newNextToken = encodeToken(page.get(page.size() - 1).getArn());
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        return new ListResult(page, newNextToken);
   280	    }
   281	
   282	    /**
   283	     * Encodes a pagination cursor as Base64 JSON.
   284	     */
   285	    private String encodeToken(String lastArn) {
   286	        if (lastArn == null) return null;
   287	        String json = "{\"lastArn\":\"" + lastArn + "\"}";
   288	        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(json.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    /**
   292	     * Decodes a pagination cursor from Base64 JSON.
   293	     */
   294	    private String decodeToken(String token) {
   295	        if (token == null || token.isEmpty()) return null;
   296	        try {
   297	            String json = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(token), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   298	            // Simple JSON parsing without Jackson dependency in this method
   299	            int start = json.indexOf("\"lastArn\":\"") + 11;
   300	            int end = json.indexOf("\"", start);
   301	            return json.substring(start, end);
   302	        } catch (Exception e) {
   303	            throw new AwsException("InvalidNextTokenException", "Invalid pagination token", 400);
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	
   307	    // ============ DeleteCertificate ============
   308	
   309	    public void deleteCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {
   310	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   311	
   312	        if (cert.getInUseBy() != null && !cert.getInUseBy().isEmpty()) {
   313	            throw new AwsException("ResourceInUseException",
   314	                "Certificate " + certificateArn + " is in use by: " + String.join(", ", cert.getInUseBy()), 409);
   315	        }
   316	
   317	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, cert.extractCertificateId());
   318	        store.delete(storageKey);
   319	        LOG.infov("Deleted certificate: {0}", certificateArn);
   320	    }

   322	    // ============ ImportCertificate ============
   323	
   324	    public Certificate importCertificate(String certificatePem, String privateKeyPem, String chainPem,
   325	                                          String existingArn, Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   326	        logSecurityWarningOnce();
   327	        // Parse and validate certificate
   328	        X509Certificate x509Cert;
   329	        try {
   330	            x509Cert = certificateGenerator.parseCertificate(certificatePem);
   331	            certificateGenerator.validateCertificate(x509Cert);
   332	        } catch (Exception e) {
   333	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid certificate: " + e.getMessage(), 400);
   334	        }
   335	
   336	        // Parse and validate private key
   337	        try {
   338	            certificateGenerator.parsePrivateKey(privateKeyPem);
   339	        } catch (Exception e) {
   340	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid private key: " + e.getMessage(), 400);
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        if (tags != null) {
   344	            validateTags(tags);
   345	        }
   346	
   347	        String certId;
   348	        String arn;
   349	
   350	        if (existingArn != null && !existingArn.isEmpty()) {
   351	            // Re-import
   352	            Certificate existing = getCertificateByArn(existingArn, region);
   353	            certId = existing.extractCertificateId();
   354	            arn = existingArn;
   355	        } else {
   356	            certId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   357	            arn = buildCertificateArn(region, certId);
   358	        }
   359	
   360	        Instant now = Instant.now();
   361	        KeyAlgorithm keyAlg = certificateGenerator.detectKeyAlgorithm(x509Cert.getPublicKey());
   362	
   363	        Certificate cert = new Certificate();
   364	        cert.setArn(arn);
   365	        cert.setDomainName(extractCommonName(x509Cert));
   366	        cert.setStatus(CertificateStatus.ISSUED);
   367	        cert.setType(CertificateType.IMPORTED);
   368	        cert.setCreatedAt(existingArn == null ? now : null);
   369	        cert.setImportedAt(now);
   370	        cert.setIssuedAt(now);
   371	        cert.setNotBefore(x509Cert.getNotBefore().toInstant());
   372	        cert.setNotAfter(x509Cert.getNotAfter().toInstant());
   373	        cert.setSerial(x509Cert.getSerialNumber().toString());
   374	        cert.setSubject(x509Cert.getSubjectX500Principal().getName());
   375	        cert.setIssuer(x509Cert.getIssuerX500Principal().getName());
   376	        cert.setKeyAlgorithm(keyAlg);
   377	        cert.setSignatureAlgorithm(x509Cert.getSigAlgName());

   390	    // ============ ExportCertificate ============
   391	
   392	    public Certificate exportCertificate(String certificateArn, String passphraseBase64, String region) {
   393	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   394	
   395	        if (!cert.canExport()) {
   396	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   397	                "Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED", 400);
   398	        }
   399	
   400	        String passphrase;
   401	        try {
   402	            passphrase = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(passphraseBase64));
   403	        } catch (Exception e) {
   404	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid passphrase encoding", 400);
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        if (passphrase.length() < 4) {
   408	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Passphrase must be at least 4 characters", 400);
   409	        }
   410	
   411	        // Encrypt the private key
   412	        String encryptedKey = certificateGenerator.encryptPrivateKey(cert.getPrivateKey(), passphrase);
   413	
   414	        // Return certificate with encrypted private key
   415	        Certificate exportCert = new Certificate();
   416	        exportCert.setCertificateBody(cert.getCertificateBody());
   417	        exportCert.setCertificateChain(cert.getCertificateChain());
   418	        exportCert.setPrivateKey(encryptedKey);
   419	        return exportCert;
   420	    }

   424	    public void addTagsToCertificate(String certificateArn, Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   425	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   426	        validateTags(tags);
   427	
   428	        Map<String, String> currentTags = cert.getTags() != null ? new HashMap<>(cert.getTags()) : new HashMap<>();
   429	        currentTags.putAll(tags);
   430	
   431	        if (currentTags.size() > MAX_TAGS) {
   432	            throw new AwsException("TooManyTagsException",
   433	                "Certificate cannot have more than " + MAX_TAGS + " tags", 400);
   434	        }
   435	
   436	        cert.setTags(currentTags);
   437	        store.put(regionKey(region, cert.extractCertificateId()), cert);
   438	    }

   440	    public Map<String, String> listTagsForCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {

   442	        return cert.getTags() != null ? new HashMap<>(cert.getTags()) : new HashMap<>();
   443	    }
   444	
   445	    public void removeTagsFromCertificate(String certificateArn, List<Map<String, String>> tagSpecs, String region) {
   446	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   447	        Map<String, String> currentTags = cert.getTags() != null ? new HashMap<>(cert.getTags()) : new HashMap<>();
   448	
   449	        for (Map<String, String> spec : tagSpecs) {
   450	            String key = spec.get("Key");
   451	            String value = spec.get("Value");
   452	            if (key != null) {
   453	                if (value == null) {
   454	                    // Remove by key only
   455	                    currentTags.remove(key);
   456	                } else {
   457	                    // Remove only if value matches
   458	                    if (value.equals(currentTags.get(key))) {
   459	                        currentTags.remove(key);
   460	                    }
   461	                }
   462	            }
   463	        }
   464	
   465	        cert.setTags(currentTags);
   466	        store.put(regionKey(region, cert.extractCertificateId()), cert);
   467	    }

   500	     *
   501	     * @param token The idempotency token
   502	     * @param region AWS region
   503	     * @param requestHash Hash of current request parameters for validation
   504	     * @return Optional containing the certificate if token is valid and not expired
   505	     * @throws AwsException if token exists but parameters don't match (IdempotencyTokenException)
   506	     */
   507	    private Optional<Certificate> findByIdempotencyToken(String token, String region, int requestHash) {
   508	        String indexKey = region + "::" + token;
   509	        IdempotencyTokenEntry entry = idempotencyTokenIndex.get(indexKey);
   510	
   511	        if (entry == null) {
   512	            return Optional.empty();
   513	        }
   514	
   515	        // Lazy expiration: remove expired entries on lookup
   516	        if (entry.isExpired()) {
   517	            idempotencyTokenIndex.remove(indexKey);
   518	            return Optional.empty();
   519	        }
   520	
   521	        // Validate request parameters match
   522	        if (entry.requestHash() != requestHash) {
   523	            throw new AwsException("IdempotencyException",
   524	                "An idempotency token was used with a request that does not match a previous request " +
   525	                "that used that token.", 400);
   526	        }
   527	
   528	        String certId = extractCertificateIdFromArn(entry.arn());
   529	        return store.get(regionKey(region, certId));
   530	    }
   531	
   532	    /**
   533	     * Computes a hash of request parameters for idempotency validation.
   534	     * Parameters include: domainName, SANs (order-independent), keyAlgorithm.
   535	     */
   536	    private int computeRequestHash(String domainName, List<String> sans, KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm) {
   537	        return Objects.hash(
   538	            domainName,
   539	            sans != null ? new HashSet<>(sans) : null,
   540	            keyAlgorithm
   541	        );
   542	    }
   543	
   544	    private void validateDomainName(String domainName) {
   545	        if (domainName == null || domainName.isEmpty()) {
   546	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Domain name cannot be empty", 400);
   547	        }
   548	        if (domainName.length() > MAX_DOMAIN_LENGTH) {
   549	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   550	                "Domain name cannot exceed " + MAX_DOMAIN_LENGTH + " characters", 400);
   551	        }
   552	    }
   553	
   554	    private void validateSans(List<String> sans) {
   555	        if (sans != null && sans.size() > MAX_SANS) {
   556	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   557	                "Cannot have more than " + MAX_SANS + " subject alternative names", 400);
   558	        }
   559	    }
   560	
   561	    private void validateTags(Map<String, String> tags) {
   562	        if (tags == null) return;
   563	
   564	        // Check total number of tags
   565	        if (tags.size() > MAX_TAGS) {
   566	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   567	                "Cannot have more than " + MAX_TAGS + " tags", 400);
   568	        }
   569	
   570	        for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : tags.entrySet()) {
   571	            String key = entry.getKey();
   572	            String value = entry.getValue();
   573	
   574	            if (key == null || key.isEmpty() || key.length() > MAX_TAG_KEY_LENGTH) {
   575	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   576	                    "Tag key must be 1-" + MAX_TAG_KEY_LENGTH + " characters", 400);
   577	            }
   578	            if (key.toLowerCase().startsWith("aws:")) {
   579	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   580	                    "Tag key cannot start with 'aws:'", 400);
   581	            }
   582	            if (value != null && value.length() > MAX_TAG_VALUE_LENGTH) {
   583	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   584	                    "Tag value cannot exceed " + MAX_TAG_VALUE_LENGTH + " characters", 400);
   585	            }
   586	        }
   587	    }
   588	
   589	    /**
   590	     * Generates domain validation options with status based on certificate type.
   591	     * Private certificates have SUCCESS status immediately; public certificates
   592	     * start with PENDING_VALIDATION until DNS/email validation completes.
   593	     */
   594	    private DomainValidation generateDomainValidation(String domain, ValidationMethod method, CertificateType type) {
   595	        String validationToken = generateValidationToken(domain);
   596	        ResourceRecord resourceRecord = new ResourceRecord(
   597	            "_" + validationToken.substring(0, 32) + "." + domain + ".",
   598	            "CNAME",
   599	            "_" + validationToken.substring(32) + ".acm-validations.aws."
   600	        );

    65	    /**
    66	     * Generates a self-signed X.509 certificate for local emulation.
    67	     *
    68	     * <p>Note: RSA key generation (especially 4096-bit) can take 100-500ms.
    69	     * In production emulator usage, consider moving this to a worker thread
    70	     * or using virtual threads for concurrent certificate generation.</p>
    71	     */
    72	    public GeneratedCertificate generateCertificate(String domainName, List<String> sans, KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm) {
    73	        try {
    74	            KeyPair keyPair = generateKeyPair(keyAlgorithm);
    75	
    76	            Instant now = Instant.now();
    77	            Instant notBefore = now;
    78	            Instant notAfter = now.plus(365, ChronoUnit.DAYS);
    79	
    80	            BigInteger serial = new BigInteger(128, SECURE_RANDOM);
    81	            String subjectDn = "CN=" + domainName;
    82	
    83	            X500Name issuer = new X500Name(ISSUER_DN);
    84	            X500Name subject = new X500Name(subjectDn);
    85	
    86	            String signatureAlgorithm = keyAlgorithm.getAlgorithm().equals("EC")
    87	                ? "SHA512withECDSA"
    88	                : "SHA512WithRSA";
    89	
    90	            X509v3CertificateBuilder certBuilder = new JcaX509v3CertificateBuilder(
    91	                issuer,
    92	                serial,
    93	                Date.from(notBefore),
    94	                Date.from(notAfter),
    95	                subject,
    96	                keyPair.getPublic()
    97	            );
    98	
    99	            // Add Subject Alternative Names
   100	            List<GeneralName> sanList = new ArrayList<>();
   101	            sanList.add(new GeneralName(GeneralName.dNSName, domainName));
   102	            if (sans != null) {
   103	                for (String san : sans) {
   104	                    if (!san.equals(domainName)) {
   105	                        sanList.add(new GeneralName(GeneralName.dNSName, san));
   106	                    }
   107	                }
   108	            }
   109	            GeneralNames generalNames = new GeneralNames(sanList.toArray(new GeneralName[0]));
   110	            certBuilder.addExtension(Extension.subjectAlternativeName, false, generalNames);
   111	
   112	            // Add Key Usage
   113	            certBuilder.addExtension(
   114	                Extension.keyUsage,
   115	                true,
   116	                new KeyUsage(KeyUsage.digitalSignature | KeyUsage.keyEncipherment)
   117	            );
   118	
   119	            // Add Basic Constraints (not a CA)
   120	            certBuilder.addExtension(
   121	                Extension.basicConstraints,
   122	                true,
   123	                new BasicConstraints(false)
   124	            );
   125	
   126	            // Self-signed certificate for local emulation - signed with subject's own private key
   127	            // Real AWS ACM certificates are signed by Amazon's CA hierarchy
   128	            ContentSigner signer = new JcaContentSignerBuilder(signatureAlgorithm)
   129	                .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME)
   130	                .build(keyPair.getPrivate());
   131	
   132	            X509CertificateHolder certHolder = certBuilder.build(signer);
   133	            X509Certificate cert = new JcaX509CertificateConverter()
   134	                .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME)
   135	                .getCertificate(certHolder);
   136	
   137	            String certPem = toPem(cert);
   138	            String keyPem = toPem(keyPair.getPrivate());
   139	
   140	            return new GeneratedCertificate(
   141	                certPem,
   142	                keyPem,
   143	                serial.toString(),
   144	                notBefore,
   145	                notAfter,

   148	                signatureAlgorithm
   149	            );

   151	        } catch (Exception e) {
   152	            LOG.error("Failed to generate certificate", e);
   153	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Certificate generation failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   154	        }

   157	    private KeyPair generateKeyPair(KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm) throws Exception {
   158	        KeyPairGenerator keyGen;
   159	        if ("EC".equals(keyAlgorithm.getAlgorithm())) {
   160	            keyGen = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("EC", BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   161	            keyGen.initialize(new ECGenParameterSpec(keyAlgorithm.getCurveName()), SECURE_RANDOM);
   162	        } else {
   163	            keyGen = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("RSA", BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   164	            keyGen.initialize(keyAlgorithm.getKeySize(), SECURE_RANDOM);
   165	        }
   166	        return keyGen.generateKeyPair();
   167	    }

   169	    private String toPem(Object obj) throws Exception {
   170	        StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
   171	        try (JcaPEMWriter pemWriter = new JcaPEMWriter(sw)) {
   172	            pemWriter.writeObject(obj);
   173	        }
   174	        return sw.toString();
   175	    }

   177	    /**
   178	     * Encrypts a private key using AES-256-CBC (replacing deprecated Triple-DES).
   179	     *
   180	     * @param privateKeyPem The private key in PEM format
   181	     * @param passphrase The passphrase for encryption
   182	     * @return Encrypted private key in PEM format

   184	    public String encryptPrivateKey(String privateKeyPem, String passphrase) {
   185	        try {
   186	            PrivateKey privateKey = parsePrivateKey(privateKeyPem);

   188	            // Use AES-256-CBC instead of deprecated Triple-DES
   189	            JcePKCSPBEOutputEncryptorBuilder encryptorBuilder = new JcePKCSPBEOutputEncryptorBuilder(
   190	                NISTObjectIdentifiers.id_aes256_CBC

   194	            PKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfoBuilder pkcs8Builder = new JcaPKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfoBuilder(privateKey);
   195	            PKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfo encryptedInfo = pkcs8Builder.build(
   196	                encryptorBuilder.build(passphrase.toCharArray())
   197	            );
   198	
   199	            StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
   200	            try (JcaPEMWriter pemWriter = new JcaPEMWriter(sw)) {
   201	                pemWriter.writeObject(encryptedInfo);
   202	            }
   203	            return sw.toString();
   204	
   205	        } catch (Exception e) {
   206	            LOG.error("Failed to encrypt private key", e);
   207	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Private key encryption failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   208	        }
   209	    }

   211	    public X509Certificate parseCertificate(String certPem) {
   212	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(certPem))) {
   213	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   214	            if (obj instanceof X509CertificateHolder holder) {
   215	                return new JcaX509CertificateConverter()
   216	                    .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME)
   217	                    .getCertificate(holder);
   218	            }
   219	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid certificate PEM format");
   220	        } catch (Exception e) {
   221	            LOG.error("Failed to parse certificate", e);
   222	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Certificate parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   223	        }
   224	    }
   225	
   226	    public PrivateKey parsePrivateKey(String keyPem) {
   227	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(keyPem))) {
   228	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   229	            JcaPEMKeyConverter converter = new JcaPEMKeyConverter()
   230	                .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   231	
   232	            if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.openssl.PEMKeyPair pemKeyPair) {
   233	                return converter.getKeyPair(pemKeyPair).getPrivate();
   234	            } else if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.asn1.pkcs.PrivateKeyInfo pkInfo) {
   235	                return converter.getPrivateKey(pkInfo);
   236	            }
   237	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid private key PEM format");
   238	        } catch (Exception e) {
   239	            LOG.error("Failed to parse private key", e);
   240	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Private key parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   241	        }
   242	    }
   243	
   244	    public void validateCertificate(X509Certificate cert) {
   245	        try {
   246	            cert.checkValidity();
   247	        } catch (Exception e) {
   248	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Certificate validation failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   249	        }
   250	    }
   251	
   252	    public KeyAlgorithm detectKeyAlgorithm(PublicKey publicKey) {
   253	        String algorithm = publicKey.getAlgorithm();
   254	        if ("RSA".equals(algorithm)) {
   255	            try {
   256	                java.security.interfaces.RSAPublicKey rsaKey = (java.security.interfaces.RSAPublicKey) publicKey;
   257	                int keySize = rsaKey.getModulus().bitLength();
   258	                return switch (keySize) {
   259	                    case 1024 -> KeyAlgorithm.RSA_1024;
   260	                    case 3072 -> KeyAlgorithm.RSA_3072;
   261	                    case 4096 -> KeyAlgorithm.RSA_4096;
   262	                    default -> KeyAlgorithm.RSA_2048;
   263	                };
   264	            } catch (Exception e) {
   265	                return KeyAlgorithm.RSA_2048;
   266	            }
   267	        } else if ("EC".equals(algorithm)) {
   268	            try {
   269	                java.security.interfaces.ECPublicKey ecKey = (java.security.interfaces.ECPublicKey) publicKey;
   270	                int fieldSize = ecKey.getParams().getCurve().getField().getFieldSize();
   271	                return switch (fieldSize) {
   272	                    case 384 -> KeyAlgorithm.EC_secp384r1;
   273	                    case 521 -> KeyAlgorithm.EC_secp521r1;
   274	                    default -> KeyAlgorithm.EC_prime256v1;
   275	                };
   276	            } catch (Exception e) {
   277	                return KeyAlgorithm.EC_prime256v1;
   278	            }
   279	        }
   280	        return KeyAlgorithm.RSA_2048;
   281	    }

   252	
   253	    public boolean isExpired() {
   254	        return notAfter != null && Instant.now().isAfter(notAfter);
   255	    }
   256	
   257	    public boolean canExport() {
   258	        return type == CertificateType.PRIVATE ||
   259	               (certOptions != null && "ENABLED".equals(certOptions.export()));
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    public String extractCertificateId() {
   263	        if (arn == null) return null;
   264	        int lastSlash = arn.lastIndexOf('/');
   265	        return lastSlash >= 0 ? arn.substring(lastSlash + 1) : arn;
   266	    }
   267	}

Now let me understand the issues better. There are two bugs:

1. **Import bug**: The AWS CLI base64-encodes blobs per JSON 1.1 spec, but the handler is reading `Certificate` and `PrivateKey` as plain text. When `aws acm import-certificate` with `fileb://` is used, the CLI base64-encodes the certificate and private key, but the ACM handler is not decoding them.

2. **Export bug**: Imported certificates have type `IMPORTED`, but `canExport()` only allows `PRIVATE` type or when `certOptions.export()` is "ENABLED". Imported certificates should also be exportable.

Let me check how the AWS JSON 1.1 protocol handles binary data

    18	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.HttpHeaders;

    20	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * Generic dispatcher for all AWS services that use the application/x-amz-json-1.1 protocol.
    24	 * Routes requests to the appropriate service handler based on the X-Amz-Target header prefix.
    25	 * <p>
    26	 * Currently supported services:
    27	 * - SSM (AmazonSSM.*)
    28	 * - EventBridge (AmazonEventBridge.*)
    29	 * - CloudWatch Logs (Logs_20140328.*)
    30	 */
    31	@Path("/")
    32	public class AwsJson11Controller {
    33	
    34	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(AwsJson11Controller.class);
    35	
    36	    private static final String SSM_TARGET_PREFIX = "AmazonSSM.";
    37	    private static final String EVENTBRIDGE_TARGET_PREFIX = "AWSEvents.";
    38	    private static final String LOGS_TARGET_PREFIX = "Logs_20140328.";
    39	    private static final String SECRETS_MANAGER_TARGET_PREFIX = "secretsmanager.";
    40	    private static final String KINESIS_TARGET_PREFIX = "Kinesis_20131202.";
    41	    private static final String APIGW_V2_TARGET_PREFIX = "AmazonApiGatewayV2.";
    42	    private static final String KMS_TARGET_PREFIX = "TrentService.";
    43	    private static final String COGNITO_TARGET_PREFIX = "AWSCognitoIdentityProviderService.";
    44	    private static final String ACM_TARGET_PREFIX = "CertificateManager.";
    45	    private static final String ECS_TARGET_PREFIX = "AmazonEC2ContainerServiceV20141113.";
    46	
    47	    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    48	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    49	    private final SsmJsonHandler ssmJsonHandler;
    50	    private final EventBridgeHandler eventBridgeHandler;
    51	    private final CloudWatchLogsHandler cloudWatchLogsHandler;
    52	    private final SecretsManagerJsonHandler secretsManagerJsonHandler;
    53	    private final KinesisJsonHandler kinesisJsonHandler;
    54	    private final ApiGatewayV2JsonHandler apigwV2JsonHandler;
    55	    private final KmsJsonHandler kmsJsonHandler;
    56	    private final CognitoJsonHandler cognitoJsonHandler;
    57	    private final AcmJsonHandler acmJsonHandler;
    58	    private final EcsJsonHandler ecsJsonHandler;
    59	
    60	    @Inject
    61	    public AwsJson11Controller(ObjectMapper objectMapper, RegionResolver regionResolver,
    62	                               SsmJsonHandler ssmJsonHandler, EventBridgeHandler eventBridgeHandler,
    63	                               CloudWatchLogsHandler cloudWatchLogsHandler,
    64	                               SecretsManagerJsonHandler secretsManagerJsonHandler,
    65	                               KinesisJsonHandler kinesisJsonHandler,
    66	                               ApiGatewayV2JsonHandler apigwV2JsonHandler,
    67	                               KmsJsonHandler kmsJsonHandler, CognitoJsonHandler cognitoJsonHandler,
    68	                               AcmJsonHandler acmJsonHandler, EcsJsonHandler ecsJsonHandler) {
    69	        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    70	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    71	        this.ssmJsonHandler = ssmJsonHandler;
    72	        this.eventBridgeHandler = eventBridgeHandler;
    73	        this.cloudWatchLogsHandler = cloudWatchLogsHandler;
    74	        this.secretsManagerJsonHandler = secretsManagerJsonHandler;
    75	        this.kinesisJsonHandler = kinesisJsonHandler;
    76	        this.apigwV2JsonHandler = apigwV2JsonHandler;
    77	        this.kmsJsonHandler = kmsJsonHandler;
    78	        this.cognitoJsonHandler = cognitoJsonHandler;
    79	        this.acmJsonHandler = acmJsonHandler;
    80	        this.ecsJsonHandler = ecsJsonHandler;
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    @POST
    84	    @Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.1")
    85	    @Produces("application/x-amz-json-1.1")
    86	    public Response handle(
    87	            @HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target,
    88	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
    89	            String body) {
    90	
    91	        if (target == null) {
    92	            return null;
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        String prefix;
    96	        String serviceName;
    97	
    98	        if (target.startsWith(SSM_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    99	            prefix = SSM_TARGET_PREFIX;
   100	            serviceName = "SSM";
   101	        } else if (target.startsWith(EVENTBRIDGE_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   102	            prefix = EVENTBRIDGE_TARGET_PREFIX;
   103	            serviceName = "EventBridge";
   104	        } else if (target.startsWith(LOGS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   105	            prefix = LOGS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   106	            serviceName = "Logs";
   107	        } else if (target.startsWith(SECRETS_MANAGER_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   108	            prefix = SECRETS_MANAGER_TARGET_PREFIX;
   109	            serviceName = "SecretsManager";
   110	        } else if (target.startsWith(KINESIS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   111	            prefix = KINESIS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   112	            serviceName = "Kinesis";
   113	        } else if (target.startsWith(APIGW_V2_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   114	            prefix = APIGW_V2_TARGET_PREFIX;
   115	            serviceName = "ApiGatewayV2";
   116	        } else if (target.startsWith(KMS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   117	            prefix = KMS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   118	            serviceName = "KMS";
   119	        } else if (target.startsWith(COGNITO_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   120	            prefix = COGNITO_TARGET_PREFIX;
   121	            serviceName = "Cognito";
   122	        } else if (target.startsWith(ACM_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   123	            prefix = ACM_TARGET_PREFIX;
   124	            serviceName = "ACM";
   125	        } else if (target.startsWith(ECS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   126	            prefix = ECS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   127	            serviceName = "ECS";
   128	        } else {
   129	            return JsonErrorResponseUtils.createUnknownOperationErrorResponse(target);
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        String action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   133	        LOG.infov("AwsJson11Controller {0} action: {1}", serviceName, action);
   134	
   135	        try {
   136	            JsonNode request = objectMapper.readTree(body);
   137	            String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   138	
   139	            return switch (serviceName) {
   140	                case "SSM" -> ssmJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   141	                case "EventBridge" -> eventBridgeHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   142	                case "Logs" -> cloudWatchLogsHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   143	                case "SecretsManager" -> secretsManagerJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   144	                case "Kinesis" -> kinesisJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   145	                case "ApiGatewayV2" -> apigwV2JsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   146	                case "KMS" -> kmsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   147	                case "Cognito" -> cognitoJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   148	                case "ACM" -> acmJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   149	                case "ECS" -> ecsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   150	                default -> null;
   151	            };
   152	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   153	            return JsonErrorResponseUtils.createErrorResponse(e);
   154	        } catch (Exception e) {
   155	            LOG.errorf("Error processing %s request", serviceName, e);
   156	            return JsonErrorResponseUtils.createErrorResponse(e);
   157	        }
   158	    }
   159

   266	            .header("X-Amz-Target", "CertificateManager.RequestCertificate")
   267	            .contentType(ACM_CONTENT_TYPE)
   268	            .body("""
   269	                {
   270	                    "DomainName": "aws-tag.example.com",
   271	                    "Tags": [{"Key": "aws:reserved", "Value": "test"}]
   272	                }
   273	                """)
   274	        .when()
   275	            .post("/")
   276	        .then()
   277	            .statusCode(400)
   278	            .body("__type", equalTo("ValidationException"));
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    @Test
   282	    void emptyTagKeyFails() {
   283	        given()
   284	            .header("X-Amz-Target", "CertificateManager.AddTagsToCertificate")
   285	            .contentType(ACM_CONTENT_TYPE)
   286	            .body("""
   287	                {
   288	                    "CertificateArn": "arn:aws:acm:us-east-1:123456789012:certificate/test",
   289	                    "Tags": [{"Key": "", "Value": "test"}]
   290	                }
   291	                """)
   292	        .when()
   293	            .post("/")
   294	        .then()
   295	            .statusCode(anyOf(equalTo(400), equalTo(404)));
   296	    }
   297	
   298	    // ==================== Key Algorithm Tests ====================
   299	
   300	    @Test
   301	    void allKeyAlgorithmsSupported() {
   302	        String[] algorithms = {"RSA_2048", "RSA_3072", "RSA_4096", "EC_prime256v1", "EC_secp384r1", "EC_secp521r1"};
   303	
   304	        for (String algo : algorithms) {
   305	            given()
   306	                .header("X-Amz-Target", "CertificateManager.RequestCertificate")
   307	                .contentType(ACM_CONTENT_TYPE)
   308	                .body("""
   309	                    {
   310	                        "DomainName": "%s.example.com",
   311	                        "KeyAlgorithm": "%s"
   312	                    }
   313	                    """.formatted(algo.toLowerCase().replace("_", "-"), algo))
   314	            .when()
   315	                .post("/")
   316	            .then()
   317	                .statusCode(200)
   318	                .body("CertificateArn", startsWith("arn:aws:acm:"));
   319	        }
   320	    }
   321	}

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/reproduce.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
set -e

echo "=== Generating test certs ==="
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/key.pem -out /tmp/cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null

echo ""
echo "=== Test 1: Import with plain text PEM (direct HTTP) ==="
echo "This should work..."
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}"

echo ""
echo ""
echo "=== Test 2: Import with base64-encoded cert/key (simulating AWS CLI) ==="
# The AWS CLI base64-encodes blobs when using fileb://
CERT_B64=$(base64 -w0 /tmp/cert.pem)
KEY_B64=$(base64 -w0 /tmp/key.pem)
echo "Base64 encoded cert: $CERT_B64"
echo ""
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"${CERT_B64}\",\"PrivateKey\":\"${KEY_B64}\"}"

echo ""
echo ""
echo "=== Test 3: Export of imported cert ==="
# First import via plain text to get an ARN
ARN=$(curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}" \
  | jq -r .CertificateArn)

echo "Imported cert ARN: $ARN"
echo ""

# Now try to export it
PASSPHRASE_B64=$(echo -n "test-passphrase" | base64 -w0)
echo "Trying to export with passphrase (base64): $PASSPHRASE_B64"
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ExportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"CertificateArn\":\"${ARN}\",\"Passphrase\":\"${PASSPHRASE_B64}\"}"
echo ""
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/reproduce.sh
echo "Script created"

2026-05-30 06:32:53,531 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-248 - 💭 THOUGHT
There's a Java version mismatch for the tests, but the source code is what we need to fix. Let me focus on the two issues:

1. **Import bug**: The `AcmJsonHandler.handleImportCertificate` reads `Certificate` and `PrivateKey` as plain text. But when the AWS CLI sends requests with `fileb://`, it base64-encodes the data. According to the [AWS JSON 1.1 protocol](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/acm/latest/APIReference/API_ImportCertificate.html), the `Certificate`, `PrivateKey`, and `CertificateChain` fields are base64-encoded blobs.

2. **Export bug**: The `canExport()` method in `Certificate.java` only allows export for `PRIVATE` type or when `certOptions.export()` is `"ENABLED"`. Imported certificates should also be exportable.

Let me verify my understanding by checking the AWS documentation for these APIs:

Now I have a clear picture. Let me look at the AWS API documentation for ImportCertificate. According to the [AWS ACM ImportCertificate API](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/acm/latest/APIReference/API_ImportCertificate.html), the `Certificate`, `PrivateKey`, and `CertificateChain` parameters are base64-encoded binary blobs.

Looking at how KMS handles this (e.g., `KmsJsonHandler.java` line 88: `Base64.getDecoder().decode(request.path("Plaintext").asText())`), we need to do the same in ACM.

Now let me fix both issues:

**Issue 1: ImportCertificate - base64 decode**
The `handleImportCertificate` method in `AcmJsonHandler.java` needs to base64-decode the `Certificate`, `PrivateKey`, and `CertificateChain` fields.

**Issue 2: ExportCertificate - allow IMPORTED type**
The `canExport()` method in `Certificate.java` should also allow `IMPORTED` type certificates to be exported.

    /**
     * Decodes a base64-encoded blob field, with fallback for plain-text PEM.
     *
     * <p>The AWS JSON 1.1 protocol specifies that binary blob fields (like Certificate,
     * PrivateKey, CertificateChain) are base64-encoded. However, some SDKs or direct HTTP
     * calls may send the raw PEM text. This method detects base64 encoding and decodes
     * accordingly.</p>
     */
    private String decodeBlob(String value, String fieldName) {
        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
            return value;
        }
        // If the value looks like PEM (starts with "-----BEGIN"), it'"'"'s already plain text
        if (value.startsWith("-----BEGIN")) {
            return value;
        }
        // Otherwise, try to base64-decode it
        try {
            byte[] decoded = java.util.Base64.getDecoder().decode(value);
            return new String(decoded, java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            // Not valid base64 - return as-is (it might be plain text with escaped newlines)
            return value;
        }
    }'

   211	    public X509Certificate parseCertificate(String certPem) {
   212	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(certPem))) {
   213	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   214	            if (obj instanceof X509CertificateHolder holder) {
   215	                return new JcaX509CertificateConverter()
   216	                    .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME)
   217	                    .getCertificate(holder);
   218	            }
   219	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid certificate PEM format");
   220	        } catch (Exception e) {
   221	            LOG.error("Failed to parse certificate", e);
   222	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Certificate parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   223	        }
   224	    }
   225	
   226	    public PrivateKey parsePrivateKey(String keyPem) {
   227	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(keyPem))) {
   228	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   229	            JcaPEMKeyConverter converter = new JcaPEMKeyConverter()
   230	                .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   231	
   232	            if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.openssl.PEMKeyPair pemKeyPair) {
   233	                return converter.getKeyPair(pemKeyPair).getPrivate();
   234	            } else if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.asn1.pkcs.PrivateKeyInfo pkInfo) {
   235	                return converter.getPrivateKey(pkInfo);
   236	            }
   237	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid private key PEM format");
   238	        } catch (Exception e) {
   239	            LOG.error("Failed to parse private key", e);
   240	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Private key parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   241	        }
   242	    }

The PEM parser in BouncyCastle should handle both `\n` and actual newlines. But there's a subtlety: when the JSON has `\\n` (escaped newlines in JSON), Jackson will convert them to actual `\n` characters in the Java string. So the PEM should be properly formatted.

However, I want to make sure the `decodeBlob` method handles the case where the value contains `\n` escape sequences from direct JSON (the workaround mentioned in the PR description). Let me think about this:

- When using `curl` with direct JSON, the `\n` in the PEM get escaped as `\\n` in the JSON string, which Jackson correctly converts to actual newline characters in the Java string. So the Java string would start with `-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----\n...` which starts with `-----BEGIN`, so it won't be base64-decoded. Good.

- When using AWS CLI with `fileb://`, the CLI base64-encodes the file content and sends it as a JSON string. So the Java string will be something like `LS0tLS1CRUdJTi...` which does NOT start with `-----BEGIN`, so it will be base64-decoded to get the PEM. Good.


This sends raw PEM with escaped newlines. This is the "workaround" format. The PR description says:
- Direct HTTP with PEM as plain string: WORKS
- AWS CLI base64-encodes blobs: FAILS

So the fix should make the base64-encoded version work while keeping the plain text version working.

Now the question is: should the response also be base64-encoded? According to AWS API, yes. But the test expects raw PEM. Let me re-read the test file to see if it was already updated...

Actually wait, the user said "I've already taken care of all changes to any of the test files described in the <pr_description>." This means the test files have been updated as needed. But looking at the test, it still expects raw PEM output. That's fine - for an emulator, it might be acceptable to return raw PEM for usability. Or maybe the test was written before the fix and the response should also be base64-encoded.

Let me check if the AWS API really base64-encodes the response. Looking at the AWS documentation for ExportCertificate:

> Certificate - The base64 PEM-encoded certificate.
> CertificateChain - The base64 PEM-encoded certificate chain. This does not include the certificate that you are exporting.
> PrivateKey - The encrypted private key associated with the public key in the certificate. The key is output in PKCS #8 format and is base64 PEM-encoded.

So yes, the response fields should also be base64-encoded. But the test expects raw PEM... 

Let me check the test more carefully. Maybe the test was already updated to expect base64:

```java
.body("Certificate", startsWith("-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----"))
```

This expects the certificate to START WITH `-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----`. If it were base64-encoded, it would start with something like `LS0tLS1CRUdJTi...`. So the test expects raw PEM.

But wait - maybe the test was already written to match the CURRENT (buggy) behavior and hasn't been updated for the fix? The PR description says both import and export are buggy. The user said "I've already taken care of all changes to any of the test files." So maybe the tests are already correct for the expected behavior after the fix.

Let me look at the actual AWS behavior: When AWS CLI calls export-certificate, it receives base64-encoded blobs and then decodes them. If our emulator returns raw PEM, the CLI would try to decode it as base64 and fail.

But for now, let me focus on the two bugs mentioned in the PR:
1. Import rejects base64-encoded certs
2. Export rejects imported certs

The response encoding for export is a separate concern. Let me check if there's already a test that would catch this.

Let me look at the integration test:

```java
.body("PrivateKey", startsWith("-----BEGIN ENCRYPTED PRIVATE KEY-----"));
```

This expects raw PEM. Since the PR description says the export bug is about "Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED", the fix is just about `canExport()`. The response format (raw PEM vs base64) is a separate issue that the tests don't flag.

```java
.body("Certificate", startsWith("-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----"))
.body("CertificateChain", startsWith("-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----"));
```

Again, raw PEM. So the emulator uses raw PEM in responses, which is fine for local development.

But wait - the PR description mentions that the AWS CLI fails when importing. The AWS CLI sends base64-encoded data and expects base64-encoded responses. If we return raw PEM in responses, the AWS CLI would still have issues. However, the PR description specifically mentions only two bugs:
1. Import fails with "Invalid certificate PEM format"
2. Export fails with "Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED"

So my two fixes address both bugs. The response encoding is a separate concern that may be handled elsewhere or may be acceptable for the emulator.

   154	
   155	    /**
   156	     * Decodes a base64-encoded blob field, with fallback for plain-text PEM.
   157	     *
   158	     * <p>The AWS JSON 1.1 protocol specifies that binary blob fields (like Certificate,
   159	     * PrivateKey, CertificateChain) are base64-encoded. However, some SDKs or direct HTTP
   160	     * calls may send the raw PEM text. This method detects base64 encoding and decodes
   161	     * accordingly.</p>
   162	     */
   163	    private String decodeBlob(String value, String fieldName) {
   164	        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
   165	            return value;
   166	        }
   167	        // If the value looks like PEM (starts with "-----BEGIN"), it's already plain text
   168	        if (value.startsWith("-----BEGIN")) {
   169	            return value;
   170	        }
   171	        // Otherwise, try to base64-decode it
   172	        try {
   173	            byte[] decoded = java.util.Base64.getDecoder().decode(value);
   174	            return new String(decoded, java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   175	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   176	            // Not valid base64 - return as-is (it might be plain text with escaped newlines)
   177	            return value;
   178	        }
   179	    }
   180

   183	        String passphrase = request.path("Passphrase").asText();

   191	        }
   192	        response.put("PrivateKey", cert.getPrivateKey());
   193	        return Response.ok(response).build();

Actually, `Base64.getDecoder()` does NOT ignore whitespace. If the base64 string has newlines (like a PEM-encoded base64), it would throw an `IllegalArgumentException`. Let me test this scenario.

Looking at how the AWS CLI sends base64: it encodes the file content and sends it as a single-line base64 string in JSON. So there shouldn't be newlines in the base64.

But what if someone encodes with `base64 -w0` (no wrapping) vs `base64` (with wrapping at 76 chars)? The AWS CLI would use the SDK which should produce clean base64.

For safety, let me use `Base64.getMimeDecoder()` which can handle whitespace, or strip whitespace before decoding.

    private String decodeBlob(String value, String fieldName) {
        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
            return value;
        }

            return value;

     * accordingly.</p>
     */
    private String decodeBlob(String value, String fieldName) {
        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
            return value;
        }
        // If the value looks like PEM (starts with "-----BEGIN"), it'"'"'s already plain text
        if (value.startsWith("-----BEGIN")) {
            return value;
        }
        // Otherwise, try to base64-decode it.
        // Use MIME decoder to handle possible whitespace/newlines in the base64 string.
        try {
            byte[] decoded = java.util.Base64.getMimeDecoder().decode(value);
            String result = new String(decoded, java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
            // Verify the decoded result is valid PEM text
            if (result.startsWith("-----BEGIN")) {
                return result;
            }
            // If decoded but doesn'"'"'t look like PEM, return original (might be a different encoding)
            return value;
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            // Not valid base64 - return as-is (it might be plain text with escaped newlines)
            return value;
        }
